This ref provides the detailed specification patterns for converting a workflow analysis into concrete code designs.\n\n## Step Graph Design\n\n### Step Definition Pattern\n\nEvery workflow operation that produces an artifact maps to a `Step`:\n\n```python\nStep(\n    id=\"step-id\",              # kebab-case, unique within pipeline\n    prompt=build_X_prompt(),   # Function from prompts.py\n    output_file=\"artifact.md\", # Relative to work_dir\n    gate=STEP_GATE,            # From gates.py\n    gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,  # BLOCKING (default) or TRAILING\n    timeout_seconds=600,       # Per-step timeout\n    inputs=[\"dep1.md\"],        # Files this step reads\n    retry_limit=1,             # How many retries on gate failure\n    model=None,                # None = use default from config\n)\n```\n\n### Gate Mode Selection\n\nChoose `GateMode` based on step criticality:\n- `BLOCKING` (default): Pipeline halts if gate fails. Use for steps whose output is consumed by downstream steps.\n- `TRAILING`: Gate evaluates asynchronously; pipeline continues. Use for quality checks that don't affect downstream data flow.\n\nRule of thumb from `resolve_gate_mode()`:\n- Release scope → always BLOCKING\n- Milestone scope → configurable\n- Task scope → TRAILING when `grace_period > 0`\n\n### Parallel Group Pattern\n\nSteps that can run concurrently are wrapped in a list:\n\n```python\nsteps = [\n    single_step_1,\n    [parallel_step_a, parallel_step_b],  # Run concurrently\n    single_step_2,                        # Waits for parallel group\n]\n```\n\nThe generic `execute_pipeline()` handles thread coordination. If using sprint-style custom executor, implement your own parallel dispatch.\n\n### Dependency Rules\n\n- Steps consume outputs of prior steps via `inputs` list\n- A step can only reference outputs from steps that precede it in the graph\n- Parallel steps within a group must not depend on each other\n- Resume logic skips steps whose output already passes their gate\n\n## Model Design Patterns\n\n### Config Model\n\nAlways extend `PipelineConfig`:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    \"\"\"Pipeline-specific configuration.\"\"\"\n    # Required: identify the input\n    source_path: Path\n\n    # Optional: control behavior\n    depth: str = \"standard\"       # quick|standard|deep\n\n    # Computed paths\n    @property\n    def results_dir(self) -> Path:\n        return self.work_dir / \"results\"\n\n    @property\n    def output_file(self, step_id: str) -> Path:\n        return self.work_dir / f\"{step_id}-output.md\"\n```\n\n### Status Enum\n\nSprint-style pipelines need richer status than generic `StepStatus`:\n\n```python\nclass StepPhaseStatus(Enum):\n    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    RUNNING = \"running\"\n    PASS = \"pass\"\n    PASS_NO_SIGNAL = \"pass_no_signal\"    # Completed but no structured report\n    PASS_NO_REPORT = \"pass_no_report\"    # Output exists but no result file\n    INCOMPLETE = \"incomplete\"             # Budget exhausted\n    HALT = \"halt\"                         # Step recommends stopping\n    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"                   # Hard timeout exceeded\n    ERROR = \"error\"                       # Process crash\n    SKIPPED = \"skipped\"                   # Skipped by config\n```\n\n### Result Model\n\nExtend `StepResult` with domain telemetry:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyStepResult(StepResult):\n    exit_code: int | None = None\n    started_at: float | None = None\n    finished_at: float | None = None\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    error_bytes: int = 0\n    # Domain-specific fields:\n    artifacts_produced: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    gate_details: dict = field(default_factory=dict)\n```\n\n### Monitor State\n\nDomain-specific signals extracted from NDJSON output:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyMonitorState:\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    last_growth_time: float = 0.0\n    events_received: int = 0\n    lines_total: int = 0\n    growth_rate_bps: float = 0.0\n    stall_seconds: float = 0.0\n    # Domain-specific signals:\n    last_step_id: str | None = None\n    current_artifact: str | None = None\n    files_changed: set = field(default_factory=set)\n```\n\n## Gate Design Patterns\n\n### Gate Criteria Tiers\n\n```python\n# Exempt: always passes (for optional/informational steps)\nEXEMPT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[],\n    min_lines=0,\n    enforcement_tier=\"EXEMPT\",\n)\n\n# Light: file exists and non-empty\nLIGHT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[],\n    min_lines=0,\n    enforcement_tier=\"LIGHT\",\n)\n\n# Standard: structural validation\nSTANDARD_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[\"title\", \"status\"],\n    min_lines=50,\n    enforcement_tier=\"STANDARD\",\n)\n\n# Strict: structural + semantic validation\nSTRICT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[\"title\", \"status\", \"convergence_score\"],\n    min_lines=100,\n    enforcement_tier=\"STRICT\",\n    semantic_checks=[\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"no_heading_gaps\",\n            check_fn=_no_heading_gaps,\n            failure_message=\"Heading hierarchy has gaps (e.g. H1→H3 without H2)\",\n        ),\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"refs_resolve\",\n            check_fn=_cross_refs_resolve,\n            failure_message=\"Cross-references do not resolve to valid targets\",\n        ),\n    ],\n)\n```\n\n### Semantic Check Functions\n\nSemantic checks are pure functions matching the `Callable[[str], bool]` signature — they take file content and return a boolean:\n\n```python\ndef _no_heading_gaps(content: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Verify heading hierarchy has no gaps (H1->H3 without H2).\"\"\"\n    # ... implementation ...\n    return True  # or False on failure\n\ndef _has_required_sections(content: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Verify all required sections are present.\"\"\"\n    required = {\"## Summary\", \"## Findings\", \"## Recommendations\"}\n    present = {line.strip() for line in content.splitlines() if line.startswith(\"## \")}\n    missing = required - present\n    return len(missing) == 0\n```\n\n### Frontmatter Validation\n\nThe shared `gate_passed()` function handles YAML frontmatter checks. Steps that produce markdown with frontmatter get automatic validation:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Diff Analysis\nstatus: complete\ndiff_points: 12\nconvergence_ready: true\n---\n```\n\n## Prompt Design Patterns\n\n### Prompt Builder Structure\n\nEach step's prompt is a function that takes inputs and returns a complete prompt string:\n\n```python\ndef build_analysis_prompt(source_path: Path, config: MyConfig) -> str:\n    return f\"\"\"Read the source file and produce a structured analysis.\n\nSource: {source_path}\nDepth: {config.depth}\n\n## Required Output Format\n\nWrite your analysis to the output file with this structure:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Analysis Report\nstatus: complete\nfinding_count: <integer>\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Summary\nBrief overview of findings.\n\n### Findings\nNumbered list of findings with evidence.\n\n### Recommendations\nActionable next steps.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nAt the end of your output, include:\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n```\nor\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n```\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### Key Prompt Rules\n\n1. **Specify output file format** — Tell Claude exactly what frontmatter fields to include\n2. **Require machine-readable markers** — `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE|HALT` for status determination\n3. **Embed input content when small** — Under ~50KB, embed directly in prompt; otherwise use `--file` args\n4. **Be explicit about sections** — Name every required section; don't leave structure to inference\n5. **Include depth/focus constraints** — If the step has configurable depth, encode it in the prompt\n\n### Input Embedding Pattern\n\n```python\ndef _embed_inputs(prompt: str, inputs: list[Path], config: MyConfig) -> tuple[str, list[str]]:\n    \"\"\"Embed small input files directly into prompt, return file args for large ones.\"\"\"\n    file_args = []\n    for input_path in inputs:\n        full_path = config.work_dir / input_path\n        if full_path.stat().st_size < 50_000:\n            content = full_path.read_text()\n            prompt += f\"\\n\\n---\\n## Input: {input_path}\\n\\n{content}\"\n        else:\n            file_args.append(str(full_path))\n    return prompt, file_args\n```\n\n## Executor Design Patterns\n\n### Sprint-Style Supervisor Loop\n\nThe sprint executor pattern provides supervised execution with monitoring. IMPORTANT: Sprint uses synchronous execution with `threading` for parallelism, NOT `async/await`. Use `time.sleep()` polling loops and `concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor` for batch dispatch.\n\n```python\ndef execute_pipeline(config: MyConfig) -> MyResult:\n    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n    verify_claude_binary()\n\n    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    logger = MyLogger(config)\n    tui = MyTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n    result = MyResult(config=config)\n    ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=config.max_turns)\n\n    # 3. Start TUI\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for step in config.steps:\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                break\n\n            # 4. Reset monitor for this step\n            monitor.reset(config.output_file(step))\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # 5. Launch Claude subprocess\n            process = ClaudeProcess(config, step)\n            process.start()\n\n            # 6. Supervision loop\n            while process.is_running():\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                state = monitor.get_state()\n\n                # Stall detection\n                if state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                # TUI update\n                tui.update(step, state)\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # 7. Classify result\n            monitor.stop()\n            status = determine_status(process.exit_code, step, config)\n\n            # 8. Record and decide\n            step_result = build_result(step, status, monitor.state)\n            result.add(step_result)\n            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n\n            if status not in (PASS, PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n                # Collect diagnostics and halt\n                diagnostics = collect_diagnostics(step_result, monitor.state)\n                write_diagnostic_report(diagnostics, config)\n                result.outcome = HALTED\n                break\n\n    finally:\n        tui.stop()\n        monitor.stop()\n        signal_handler.restore()\n\n    return result\n```\n\n### Status Classification\n\nMap every possible exit condition to a deterministic status:\n\n```python\ndef determine_status(exit_code, step, config):\n    # 1. Hard failures\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return ERROR\n\n    # 2. Check for structured result file\n    result_path = config.result_file(step)\n    if result_path.exists():\n        content = result_path.read_text()\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n            return HALT\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n            return PASS\n        return PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    # 3. Check for output without result\n    output_path = config.output_file(step)\n    if output_path.exists():\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n            return INCOMPLETE\n        return PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    # 4. No output at all\n    return ERROR\n```\n\n## Integration Patterns\n\n### main.py Registration\n\n```python\n# In src/superclaude/cli/main.py\nfrom superclaude.cli.my_pipeline import my_pipeline_group\napp.add_command(my_pipeline_group)\n```\n\n### Click Command Group\n\n```python\n@click.group(\"my-pipeline\")\ndef my_pipeline_group():\n    \"\"\"My pipeline description.\"\"\"\n    pass\n\n@my_pipeline_group.command(\"run\")\n@click.argument(\"source\")\n@click.option(\"--depth\", default=\"standard\", type=click.Choice([\"quick\", \"standard\", \"deep\"]))\n@click.option(\"--dry-run\", is_flag=True)\n@click.option(\"--max-turns\", default=25, type=int)\n@click.option(\"--model\", default=None)\n@click.option(\"--debug\", is_flag=True)\ndef run(source, depth, dry_run, max_turns, model, debug):\n    \"\"\"Execute the pipeline.\"\"\"\n    config = load_config(source, depth=depth, dry_run=dry_run, ...)\n    result = execute_pipeline(config)\n    sys.exit(0 if result.success else 1)\n```\n\n## Turn Budget Economics (from unified-audit-gating)\n\nFor pipelines with multiple Claude subprocesses, use `TurnLedger` to manage budget:\n\n```python\nfrom superclaude.cli.sprint.models import TurnLedger\n\n@dataclass\nclass MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    max_turns: int = 200\n    min_launch_allocation: int = 10\n    min_remediation_budget: int = 5\n\n# In executor:\nledger = TurnLedger(\n    initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n    minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n    minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n)\n\n# Before launching a step:\nif not ledger.can_launch():\n    result.outcome = HALTED\n    result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n    break\n\n# After step completes, count actual turns used:\nactual_turns = count_turns_from_output(output_path)\nledger.debit(actual_turns)\n\n# If step used fewer turns than allocated, credit back:\nif actual_turns < allocated:\n    ledger.credit(allocated - actual_turns)\n```\n\n## Subprocess Isolation Pattern\n\nFor pipelines spawning child Claude sessions, use the 4-layer isolation model:\n\n```python\ndef setup_isolation(work_dir: Path) -> dict[str, str]:\n    \"\"\"Create isolated environment for child Claude subprocess.\"\"\"\n    env = os.environ.copy()\n\n    # Layer 1: Scoped work directory\n    env[\"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\"] = str(work_dir)\n\n    # Layer 2: Git ceiling (prevent escaping work_dir)\n    env[\"GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES\"] = str(work_dir.parent)\n\n    # Layer 3: Isolated plugin directory\n    plugin_dir = work_dir / \".claude-plugins\"\n    plugin_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    env[\"CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DIR\"] = str(plugin_dir)\n\n    # Layer 4: Isolated settings\n    settings_dir = work_dir / \".claude-settings\"\n    settings_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    env[\"CLAUDE_SETTINGS_DIR\"] = str(settings_dir)\n\n    return env\n```\n\n## Context Injection Pattern\n\nPrior step results feed into subsequent prompts as compressed context:\n\n```python\ndef build_step_prompt_with_context(step, prior_results: list[StepResult]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Build prompt with prior step context injected.\"\"\"\n    base_prompt = step.prompt\n\n    if not prior_results:\n        return base_prompt\n\n    context_block = \"## Prior Step Context\\n\\n\"\n    for result in prior_results[-3:]:  # Keep recent, compress older\n        context_block += result.to_context_summary(verbose=(result == prior_results[-1]))\n        context_block += \"\\n\\n\"\n\n    return f\"{base_prompt}\\n\\n{context_block}\"\n```\n\n## Resume-First Failure Output Pattern\n\nOn halt, generate actionable resume information:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyResult:\n    # ... other fields ...\n\n    def resume_command(self) -> str | None:\n        \"\"\"Generate CLI command to resume from failure point.\"\"\"\n        if not self.halt_step:\n            return None\n        remaining = [r.step.id for r in self.step_results\n                     if r.status == MyStatus.PENDING]\n        return (\n            f\"superclaude {CLI_NAME} run \"\n            f\"--resume --start {self.halt_step} \"\n            f\"--max-turns {self.suggested_resume_budget}\"\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def suggested_resume_budget(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Estimate turns needed to complete remaining work.\"\"\"\n        remaining_steps = sum(1 for r in self.step_results\n                              if r.status in (MyStatus.PENDING, MyStatus.INCOMPLETE))\n        return remaining_steps * 25  # Default allocation per step\n```\n\n## Pure-Programmatic Step Execution\n\nNot all steps need Claude. Pure-programmatic steps run as direct Python function calls:\n\n```python\ndef execute_step(step, config):\n    \"\"\"Route step to appropriate executor.\"\"\"\n    if step.prompt == \"\":\n        # Pure programmatic — run directly\n        return run_programmatic_step(step, config)\n    else:\n        # Claude-assisted — launch subprocess\n        return run_claude_step(step, config)\n\ndef run_programmatic_step(step, config) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a pure-programmatic step without Claude.\"\"\"\n    started = time.time()\n    try:\n        # Call the step's implementation function\n        PROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS[step.id](config)\n        return StepResult(step=step, status=StepStatus.PASS,\n                         started_at=started, finished_at=time.time())\n    except Exception as e:\n        return StepResult(step=step, status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n                         gate_failure_reason=str(e),\n                         started_at=started, finished_at=time.time())\n```\n\n## Gate Display State Machine (for TUI)\n\nModel gate states as explicit transitions for richer UX:\n\n```python\nclass GateDisplayState(Enum):\n    NONE = \"none\"\n    CHECKING = \"checking\"\n    PASS = \"pass\"\n    FAIL_DEFERRED = \"fail_deferred\"\n    REMEDIATING = \"remediating\"\n    REMEDIATED = \"remediated\"\n    HALT = \"halt\"\n\n    @property\n    def icon(self) -> str:\n        return {\n            \"none\": \" \", \"checking\": \"...\",\n            \"pass\": \"ok\", \"fail_deferred\": \"!\",\n            \"remediating\": \"~\", \"remediated\": \"ok\",\n            \"halt\": \"X\",\n        }[self.value]\n```\n","numLines":591,"startLine":1,"totalLines":591}}}

Prompt\n\n```python\ndef build_structural_analysis_prompt(\n    batch_files: list[str],\n    surface_results_path: Path,\n    config: CleanupAuditConfig,\n) -> str:\n    return f\"\"\"You are an does\n2. **Imports**: Key dependencies\n3. **Exports**: Public API surface\n4. **Complexity**: Cyclomatic complexity estimate\n5. **Coverage**: Test coverage indicator\n6. **Staleness**: Last meaningful change indicator\n7. **Coupling**: Files that depend on this / files this depends on\n8. **Recommendation**: KEEP / REFACTOR / DELETE with justification\n\n## Required Output Format\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Structural Analysis — Batch\nstatus: complete\npass: structural\nfile_count: {len(batch_files)}\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\nFor each file, create a `## <filename>` section with the 8-field profile.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### 2.4 G-004: Cross-Cutting Comparison Prompt\n\n```python\ndef build_cross_cutting_prompt(\n    surface_results_path: Path,\n    structural_results_path: Path,\n    config: CleanupAuditConfig,\n) -> str:\n    return f\"\"\"You are an audit-comparator agent performing Pass 3 (cross-cutting comparison) of a repository audit.\n\n## Prior Context\n\n- Surface scan results: {surface_results_path}\n- Structural analysis results: {structural_results_path}\n\n## Task\n\nAnalyze cross-cutting concerns across the entire codebase:\n\n1. **Duplication Detection**: Identify files or code blocks that duplicate functionality\n2. **Sprawl Analysis**: Find feature sprawl — similar concepts implemented in multiple places\n3. **Consolidation Opportunities**: Recommend merges, extractions, or eliminations\n4. **Dependency Patterns**: Identify unhealthy dependency patterns (circular, deep chains)\n\n## Required Output Format\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Cross-Cutting Comparison\nstatus: complete\npass: cross-cutting\nfinding_count: <integer>\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Duplication Findings\nNumbered list with evidence (file paths, line ranges).\n\n### Sprawl Analysis\nFeature areas with redundant implementations.\n\n### Consolidation Opportunities\nActionable recommendations with estimated effort.\n\n### Dependency Issues\nProblematic dependency patterns with remediation suggestions.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### 2.5 G-005: Consolidate Findings Prompt\n\n```python\ndef build_consolidation_prompt(\n    surface_path: Path,\n    structural_path: Path,\n    cross_cutting_path: Path,\n    config: CleanupAuditConfig,\n) -> str:\n    return f\"\"\"You are an audit-consolidator agent producing the final consolidated audit report.\n\n## Prior Context\n\n- Surface scan: {surface_path}\n- Structural analysis: {structural_path}\n- Cross-cutting comparison: {cross_cutting_path}\n\n## Task\n\n1. **Merge** findings from all three passes\n2. **Deduplicate** findings that appear in multiple passes\n3. **Rank** by severity (critical > high > medium > low)\n4. **Summarize** total findings with severity distribution\n\n## Required Output Format\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Consolidated Audit Report\nstatus: complete\ntotal_findings: <integer>\nseverity_distribution:\n  critical: <integer>\n  high: <integer>\n  medium: <integer>\n  low: <integer>\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Executive Summary\nHigh-level overview of audit findings.\n\n### Findings by Severity\n#### Critical\n#### High\n#### Medium\n#### Low\n\nEach finding includes: ID, description, evidence, affected files, recommended action.\n\n### Deduplication Log\nShow which findings were merged and from which passes.\n\n### Recommendations\nPrioritized action items.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\nor\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n(if critical findings require immediate attention)\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### 2.6 G-006: Validate Claims Prompt\n\n```python\ndef build_validation_prompt(\n    consolidated_path: Path,\n    sample_findings: list[str],\n    config: CleanupAuditConfig,\n) -> str:\n    findings_list = \"\\n\".join(f\"- {f}\" for f in sample_findings)\n    return f\"\"\"You are an audit-validator agent performing spot-check validation of audit findings.\n\n## Prior Context\n\nConsolidated audit report: {consolidated_path}\n\n## Sampled Findings to Validate\n\n{findings_list}\n\n## Task\n\nFor each sampled finding:\n1. **Re-test** the claim independently using grep/read operations\n2. **Verdict**: CONFIRMED or REFUTED with evidence\n3. **Confidence**: high/medium/low\n\n## Required Output Format\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Spot-Check Validation\nstatus: complete\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Validation Results\n\n| Finding ID | Claim | Verdict | Evidence | Confidence |\n|-----------|-------|---------|----------|------------|\n| ... | ... | CONFIRMED/REFUTED | ... | ... |\n\n### Summary\n\nValidation pass rate and confidence assessment.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### 2.7 Prompt Size Assessment\n\nTotal prompt template lines: ~250 lines across 5 Claude-assisted steps.\n**Decision**: Prompts fit within the 300-line threshold. No split to `portify-prompts.md` needed.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Pure-Programmatic Step Design (FR-029)\n\n### G-001: Discover and Classify Files\n\nThis is the sole pure-programmatic step. Full Python code specification:\n\n```python\ndef run_discover_files(config: CleanupAuditConfig) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    G-001: Discover and classify files in the target repository.\n\n    Produces: {work_dir}/G-001-output.md\n    Gate: LIGHT / BLOCKING\n    \"\"\"\n    target = config.target_path.resolve()\n    output = config.work_dir / \"G-001-output.md\"\n\n    # 1. Walk the directory tree, respecting .gitignore\n    all_files = []\n    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(target):\n        # Skip hidden dirs and common ignores\n        dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if not d.startswith(\".\") and d not in {\"node_modules\", \"__pycache__\", \".git\"}]\n        for f in files:\n            rel_path = os.path.relpath(os.path.join(root, f), target)\n            ext = os.path.splitext(f)[1]\n            size = os.path.getsize(os.path.join(root, f))\n            all_files.append({\n                \"path\": rel_path,\n                \"extension\": ext,\n                \"size_bytes\": size,\n            })\n\n    # 2. Classify by extension into categories\n    categories = {\n        \"code\": {\".py\", \".ts\", \".tsx\", \".js\", \".jsx\", \".go\", \".rs\", \".java\"},\n        \"config\": {\".yaml\", \".yml\", \".json\", \".toml\", \".ini\", \".cfg\"},\n        \"docs\": {\".md\", \".rst\", \".txt\"},\n        \"test\": set(),  # Identified by path patterns\n        \"other\": set(),\n    }\n\n    for f in all_files:\n        if \"test\" in f[\"path\"].lower() or f[\"path\"].startswith(\"tests/\"):\n            f[\"category\"] = \"test\"\n        elif f[\"extension\"] in categories[\"code\"]:\n            f[\"category\"] = \"code\"\n        elif f[\"extension\"] in categories[\"config\"]:\n            f[\"category\"] = \"config\"\n        elif f[\"extension\"] in categories[\"docs\"]:\n            f[\"category\"] = \"docs\"\n        else:\n            f[\"category\"] = \"other\"\n\n    # 3. Write output\n    with open(output, \"w\") as fh:\n        fh.write(\"---\\n\")\n        fh.write(f\"title: File Discovery Inventory\\n\")\n        fh.write(f\"status: complete\\n\")\n        fh.write(f\"total_files: {len(all_files)}\\n\")\n        fh.write(\"---\\n\\n\")\n        fh.write(\"# File Inventory\\n\\n\")\n        fh.write(\"| Path | Extension | Size | Category |\\n\")\n        fh.write(\"|------|-----------|------|----------|\\n\")\n        for f in sorted(all_files, key=lambda x: x[\"path\"]):\n            fh.write(f\"| {f['path']} | {f['extension']} | {f['size_bytes']} | {f['category']} |\\n\")\n        fh.write(f\"\\n## Summary\\n\\n\")\n        for cat in [\"code\", \"test\", \"config\", \"docs\", \"other\"]:\n            count = sum(1 for f in all_files if f[\"category\"] == cat)\n            fh.write(f\"- **{cat}**: {count} files\\n\")\n```\n\n**PROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS registration**:\n```python\nPROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS = {\n    \"G-001\": run_discover_files,\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Executor Design (FR-030)\n\n### 4.1 Architecture: Sprint-Style Synchronous Supervisor\n\nThe executor follows the sprint-style supervisor loop pattern from pipeline-spec.md:\n- **Synchronous** supervisor loop (not async/await)\n- **ThreadPoolExecutor** for batch dispatch of parallel steps (S-002, S-003)\n- **time.sleep()** polling for subprocess monitoring\n- **TurnLedger** for budget management (from `superclaude.cli.sprint.models`)\n\n### 4.2 Executor Pseudocode\n\n```python\ndef execute_cleanup_audit(config: CleanupAuditConfig) -> AuditResult:\n    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n    verify_claude_binary()\n\n    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    ledger = TurnLedger(\n        initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n        minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n        minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n    )\n    result = AuditResult(config=config)\n\n    try:\n        # Step ordering follows topological sort from D-0018:\n        # G-001 → G-002 → G-003 → G-004 → G-005 → G-006\n\n        # --- G-001: Pure programmatic (discover files) ---\n        step_result = run_programmatic_step(\"G-001\", config)\n        result.add(step_result)\n        if step_result.status != AuditStepStatus.PASS:\n            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n            return result\n\n        # --- G-002: Claude-assisted batch (surface scan) ---\n        file_inventory = parse_inventory(config.work_dir / \"G-001-output.md\")\n        batches = create_batches(file_inventory, config.batch_size)\n\n        for batch_idx, batch in enumerate(batches):\n            if not ledger.can_launch():\n                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n                result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n                return result\n\n            step_result = run_claude_step(\n                step_id=f\"G-002\",\n                prompt=build_surface_scan_prompt(batch, config),\n                gate=G002_GATE,\n                gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n                config=config,\n                ledger=ledger,\n            )\n            result.add(step_result)\n            if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n                return result\n\n        # --- G-003: Claude-assisted batch (structural analysis) ---\n        review_files = extract_review_files(config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\")\n        batches = create_batches(review_files, config.batch_size)\n\n        for batch_idx, batch in enumerate(batches):\n            if not ledger.can_launch():\n                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n                return result\n\n            step_result = run_claude_step(\n                step_id=f\"G-003\",\n                prompt=build_structural_analysis_prompt(\n                    batch, config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\", config\n                ),\n                gate=G003_GATE,\n                gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n                config=config,\n                ledger=ledger,\n            )\n            result.add(step_result)\n            if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n                return result\n\n        # --- G-004: Claude-assisted single (cross-cutting) ---\n        if not ledger.can_launch():\n            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n            return result\n\n        step_result = run_claude_step(\n            step_id=\"G-004\",\n            prompt=build_cross_cutting_prompt(\n                config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\",\n                config.work_dir / \"G-003-output.md\",\n                config,\n            ),\n            gate=G004_GATE,\n            gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n            config=config,\n            ledger=ledger,\n        )\n        result.add(step_result)\n        if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n            return result\n\n        # --- G-005: Claude-assisted single (consolidate) ---\n        if not ledger.can_launch():\n            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n            return result\n\n        step_result = run_claude_step(\n            step_id=\"G-005\",\n            prompt=build_consolidation_prompt(\n                config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\",\n                config.work_dir / \"G-003-output.md\",\n                config.work_dir / \"G-004-output.md\",\n                config,\n            ),\n            gate=G005_GATE,\n            gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n            config=config,\n            ledger=ledger,\n        )\n        result.add(step_result)\n        if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n            return result\n\n        # --- G-006: Claude-assisted single (validate — TRAILING) ---\n        if not ledger.can_launch():\n            # Trailing step — budget exhaustion is advisory, not blocking\n            result.add_advisory(\"G-006 skipped: budget exhausted\")\n        else:\n            step_result = run_claude_step(\n                step_id=\"G-006\",\n                prompt=build_validation_prompt(\n                    config.work_dir / \"G-005-output.md\",\n                    sample_findings(config.work_dir / \"G-005-output.md\"),\n                    config,\n                ),\n                gate=G006_GATE,\n                gate_mode=GateMode.TRAILING,\n                config=config,\n                ledger=ledger,\n            )\n            result.add(step_result)\n            # TRAILING: pipeline continues regardless of gate result\n\n        result.outcome = \"PASSED\"\n        return result\n\n    finally:\n        signal_handler.restore()\n```\n\n### 4.3 Batch Dispatch with ThreadPoolExecutor\n\nFor steps that process batches (G-002, G-003), the executor uses `ThreadPoolExecutor` when batches are independent:\n\n```python\nfrom concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed\n\ndef execute_parallel_batches(\n    batches: list[list[str]],\n    build_prompt_fn: callable,\n    gate: GateCriteria,\n    config: CleanupAuditConfig,\n    ledger: TurnLedger,\n    max_workers: int = 3,\n) -> list[AuditStepResult]:\n    \"\"\"Execute independent batches in parallel using ThreadPoolExecutor.\"\"\"\n    results = []\n\n    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=max_workers) as executor:\n        futures = {}\n        for batch_idx, batch in enumerate(batches):\n            if not ledger.can_launch():\n                break\n            future = executor.submit(\n                run_claude_step,\n                step_id=f\"batch-{batch_idx}\",\n                prompt=build_prompt_fn(batch, config),\n                gate=gate,\n                config=config,\n                ledger=ledger,\n            )\n            futures[future] = batch_idx\n\n        for future in as_completed(futures):\n            batch_idx = futures[future]\n            result = future.result()\n            results.append(result)\n\n    return sorted(results, key=lambda r: r.batch_index)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Pattern Coverage Matrix (FR-031)\n\n### 5.1 Supported Patterns Enumeration\n\nThe 7 supported pipeline primitive patterns (from `refs/analysis-protocol.md` \"Map to Pipeline Primitives\"):\n\n| # | Pattern | Pipeline Primitive | Description |\n|---|---------|-------------------|-------------|\n| 1 | Sequential step | `Step` in step list | Single step executing in sequence |\n| 2 | Parallel operations | `list[Step]` parallel group / ThreadPoolExecutor batch | Concurrent step execution |\n| 3 | Quality gate | `GateCriteria` on Step | Output validation with tier enforcement |\n| 4 | Agent delegation | Prompt in `prompts.py` | Claude subprocess with structured prompt |\n| 5 | Scoring formula | Python function in `gates.py` | Semantic check as `Callable[[str], bool]` |\n| 6 | Status decision | `determine_status()` in executor | Exit code + signal classification |\n| 7 | Input validation | Config validation logic | Pre-flight checks and parameter validation |\n\n### 5.2 Coverage Matrix: sc-cleanup-audit-protocol\n\n| Pattern | Required by Workflow? | Covering Step Design | Coverage Status |\n|---------|----------------------|---------------------|----------------|\n| Sequential step | Yes | G-001 → G-002 → G-003 → G-004 → G-005 → G-006 (topological order) | ✅ Covered |\n| Parallel operations | Yes | G-002, G-003 use ThreadPoolExecutor batch dispatch | ✅ Covered |\n| Quality gate | Yes | All 6 steps have GateCriteria defined (D-0023) | ✅ Covered |\n| Agent delegation | Yes | G-002 through G-006 use Claude subprocess prompts | ✅ Covered |\n| Scoring formula | Yes | 7 semantic check functions defined with `Callable[[str], bool]` | ✅ Covered |\n| Status decision | Yes | `determine_status()` classifies 8 exit conditions | ✅ Covered |\n| Input validation | Yes | `CleanupAuditConfig` validates target_path, batch_size, pass_filter | ✅ Covered |\n\n**Coverage result**: 7/7 patterns covered ✅\n**Gaps detected**: 0\n**Coverage complete**: true\n\n---\n\n## 6. <integer>\n  low: <integer>\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Executive Summary\nHigh-level overview of audit findings.\n\n### Findings by Severity\n#### Critical\n#### High\n#### Medium\n#### Low\n\nEach finding includes: ID, description, evidence, affected files, recommended action.\n\n### Deduplication Log\nShow which findings were merged and from which passes.\n\n### Recommendations\nPrioritized action items.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\nor\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n(if critical findings require immediate attention)\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### 2.6 G-006: Validate Claims Prompt\n\n```python\ndef build_validation_prompt(\n    consolidated_path: Path,\n    sample_findings: list[str],\n    config: CleanupAuditConfig,\n) -> str:\n    findings_list = \"\\n\".join(f\"- {f}\" for f in sample_findings)\n    return f\"\"\"You are an audit-validator agent performing spot-check validation of audit findings.\n\n## Prior Context\n\nConsolidated audit report: {consolidated_path}\n\n## Sampled Findings to Validate\n\n{findings_list}\n\n## Task\n\nFor each sampled finding:\n1. **Re-test** the claim independently using grep/read operations\n2. **Verdict**: CONFIRMED or REFUTED with evidence\n3. **Confidence**: high/medium/low\n\n## Required Output Format\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Spot-Check Validation\nstatus: complete\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Validation Results\n\n| Finding ID | Claim | Verdict | Evidence | Confidence |\n|-----------|-------|---------|----------|------------|\n| ... | ... | CONFIRMED/REFUTED | ... | ... |\n\n### Summary\n\nValidation pass rate and confidence assessment.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### 2.7 Prompt Size Assessment\n\nTotal prompt template lines: ~250 lines across 5 Claude-assisted steps.\n**Decision**: Prompts fit within the 300-line threshold. No split to `portify-prompts.md` needed.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Pure-Programmatic Step Design (FR-029)\n\n### G-001: Discover and Classify Files\n\nThis is the sole pure-programmatic step. Full Python code specification:\n\n```python\ndef run_discover_files(config: CleanupAuditConfig) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    G-001: Discover and classify files in the target repository.\n\n    Produces: {work_dir}/G-001-output.md\n    Gate: LIGHT / BLOCKING\n    \"\"\"\n    target = config.target_path.resolve()\n    output = config.work_dir / \"G-001-output.md\"\n\n    # 1. Walk the directory tree, respecting .gitignore\n    all_files = []\n    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(target):\n        # Skip hidden dirs and common ignores\n        dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if not d.startswith(\".\") and d not in {\"node_modules\", \"__pycache__\", \".git\"}]\n        for f in files:\n            rel_path = os.path.relpath(os.path.join(root, f), target)\n            ext = os.path.splitext(f)[1]\n            size = os.path.getsize(os.path.join(root, f))\n            all_files.append({\n                \"path\": rel_path,\n                \"extension\": ext,\n                \"size_bytes\": size,\n            })\n\n    # 2. Classify by extension into categories\n    categories = {\n        \"code\": {\".py\", \".ts\", \".tsx\", \".js\", \".jsx\", \".go\", \".rs\", \".java\"},\n        \"config\": {\".yaml\", \".yml\", \".json\", \".toml\", \".ini\", \".cfg\"},\n        \"docs\": {\".md\", \".rst\", \".txt\"},\n        \"test\": set(),  # Identified by path patterns\n        \"other\": set(),\n    }\n\n    for f in all_files:\n        if \"test\" in f[\"path\"].lower() or f[\"path\"].startswith(\"tests/\"):\n            f[\"category\"] = \"test\"\n        elif f[\"extension\"] in categories[\"code\"]:\n            f[\"category\"] = \"code\"\n        elif f[\"extension\"] in categories[\"config\"]:\n            f[\"category\"] = \"config\"\n        elif f[\"extension\"] in categories[\"docs\"]:\n            f[\"category\"] = \"docs\"\n        else:\n            f[\"category\"] = \"other\"\n\n    # 3. Write output\n    with open(output, \"w\") as fh:\n        fh.write(\"---\\n\")\n        fh.write(f\"title: File Discovery Inventory\\n\")\n        fh.write(f\"status: complete\\n\")\n        fh.write(f\"total_files: {len(all_files)}\\n\")\n        fh.write(\"---\\n\\n\")\n        fh.write(\"# File Inventory\\n\\n\")\n        fh.write(\"| Path | Extension | Size | Category |\\n\")\n        fh.write(\"|------|-----------|------|----------|\\n\")\n        for f in sorted(all_files, key=lambda x: x[\"path\"]):\n            fh.write(f\"| {f['path']} | {f['extension']} | {f['size_bytes']} | {f['category']} |\\n\")\n        fh.write(f\"\\n## Summary\\n\\n\")\n        for cat in [\"code\", \"test\", \"config\", \"docs\", \"other\"]:\n            count = sum(1 for f in all_files if f[\"category\"] == cat)\n            fh.write(f\"- **{cat}**: {count} files\\n\")\n```\n\n**PROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS registration**:\n```python\nPROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS = {\n    \"G-001\": run_discover_files,\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Executor Design (FR-030)\n\n### 4.1 Architecture: Sprint-Style Synchronous Supervisor\n\nThe executor follows the sprint-style supervisor loop pattern from pipeline-spec.md:\n- **Synchronous** supervisor loop (not async/await)\n- **ThreadPoolExecutor** for batch dispatch of parallel steps (S-002, S-003)\n- **time.sleep()** polling for subprocess monitoring\n- **TurnLedger** for budget management (from `superclaude.cli.sprint.models`)\n\n### 4.2 Executor Pseudocode\n\n```python\ndef execute_cleanup_audit(config: CleanupAuditConfig) -> AuditResult:\n    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n    verify_claude_binary()\n\n    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    ledger = TurnLedger(\n        initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n        minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n        minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n    )\n    result = AuditResult(config=config)\n\n    try:\n        # Step ordering follows topological sort from D-0018:\n        # G-001 → G-002 → G-003 → G-004 → G-005 → G-006\n\n        # --- G-001: Pure programmatic (discover files) ---\n        step_result = run_programmatic_step(\"G-001\", config)\n        result.add(step_result)\n        if step_result.status != AuditStepStatus.PASS:\n            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n            return result\n\n        # --- G-002: Claude-assisted batch (surface scan) ---\n        file_inventory = parse_inventory(config.work_dir / \"G-001-output.md\")\n        batches = create_batches(file_inventory, config.batch_size)\n\n        for batch_idx, batch in enumerate(batches):\n            if not ledger.can_launch():\n                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n                result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n                return result\n\n            step_result = run_claude_step(\n                step_id=f\"G-002\",\n                prompt=build_surface_scan_prompt(batch, config),\n                gate=G002_GATE,\n                gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n                config=config,\n                ledger=ledger,\n            )\n            result.add(step_result)\n            if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n                return result\n\n        # --- G-003: Claude-assisted batch (structural analysis) ---\n        review_files = extract_review_files(config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\")\n        batches = create_batches(review_files, config.batch_size)\n\n        for batch_idx, batch in enumerate(batches):\n            if not ledger.can_launch():\n                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n                return result\n\n            step_result = run_claude_step(\n                step_id=f\"G-003\",\n                prompt=build_structural_analysis_prompt(\n                    batch, config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\", config\n                ),\n                gate=G003_GATE,\n                gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n                config=config,\n                ledger=ledger,\n            )\n            result.add(step_result)\n            if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n                return result\n\n        # --- G-004: Claude-assisted single (cross-cutting) ---\n        if not ledger.can_launch():\n            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n            return result\n\n        step_result = run_claude_step(\n            step_id=\"G-004\",\n            prompt=build_cross_cutting_prompt(\n                config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\",\n                config.work_dir / \"G-003-output.md\",\n                config,\n            ),\n            gate=G004_GATE,\n            gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n            config=config,\n            ledger=ledger,\n        )\n        result.add(step_result)\n        if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n            return result\n\n        # --- G-005: Claude-assisted single (consolidate) ---\n        if not ledger.can_launch():\n            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n            return result\n\n        step_result = run_claude_step(\n            step_id=\"G-005\",\n            prompt=build_consolidation_prompt(\n                config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\",\n                config.work_dir / \"G-003-output.md\",\n                config.work_dir / \"G-004-output.md\",\n                config,\n            ),\n            gate=G005_GATE,\n            gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n            config=config,\n            ledger=ledger,\n        )\n        result.add(step_result)\n        if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n            return result\n\n        # --- G-006: Claude-assisted single (validate — TRAILING) ---\n        if not ledger.can_launch():\n            # Trailing step — budget exhaustion is advisory, not blocking\n            result.add_advisory(\"G-006 skipped: budget exhausted\")\n        else:\n            step_result = run_claude_step(\n                step_id=\"G-006\",\n                prompt=build_validation_prompt(\n                    config.work_dir / \"G-005-output.md\",\n                    sample_findings(config.work_dir / \"G-005-output.md\"),\n                    config,\n                ),\n                gate=G006_GATE,\n                gate_mode=GateMode.TRAILING,\n                config=config,\n                ledger=ledger,\n            )\n            result.add(step_result)\n            # TRAILING: pipeline continues regardless of gate result\n\n        result.outcome = \"PASSED\"\n        return result\n\n    finally:\n        signal_handler.restore()\n```\n\n### 4.3 Batch Dispatch with ThreadPoolExecutor\n\nFor steps that process batches (G-002, G-003), the executor uses `ThreadPoolExecutor` when batches are independent:\n\n```python\nfrom concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed\n\ndef execute_parallel_batches(\n    batches: list[list[str]],\n    build_prompt_fn: callable,\n    gate: GateCriteria,\n    config: CleanupAuditConfig,\n    ledger: TurnLedger,\n    max_workers: int = 3,\n) -> list[AuditStepResult]:\n    \"\"\"Execute independent batches in parallel using ThreadPoolExecutor.\"\"\"\n    results = []\n\n    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=max_workers) as executor:\n        futures = {}\n        for batch_idx, batch in enumerate(batches):\n            if not ledger.can_launch():\n                break\n            future = executor.submit(\n                run_claude_step,\n                step_id=f\"batch-{batch_idx}\",\n                prompt=build_prompt_fn(batch, config),\n                gate=gate,\n                config=config,\n                ledger=ledger,\n            )\n            futures[future] = batch_idx\n\n        for future in as_completed(futures):\n            batch_idx = futures[future]\n            result = future.result()\n            results.append(result)\n\n    return sorted(results, key=lambda r: r.batch_index)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Pattern Coverage Matrix (FR-031)\n\n### 5.1 Supported Patterns Enumeration\n\nThe 7 supported pipeline primitive patterns (from `refs/analysis-protocol.md` \"Map to Pipeline Primitives\"):\n\n| # | Pattern | Pipeline Primitive | Description |\n|---|---------|-------------------|-------------|\n| 1 | Sequential step | `Step` in step list | Single step executing in sequence |\n| 2 | Parallel operations | `list[Step]` parallel group / ThreadPoolExecutor batch | Concurrent step execution |\n| 3 | Quality gate | `GateCriteria` on Step | Output validation with tier enforcement |\n| 4 | Agent delegation | Prompt in `prompts.py` | Claude subprocess with structured prompt |\n| 5 | Scoring formula | Python function in `gates.py` | Semantic check as `Callable[[str], bool]` |\n| 6 | Status decision | `determine_status()` in executor | Exit code + signal classification |\n| 7 | Input validation | Config validation logic | Pre-flight checks and parameter validation |\n\n### 5.2 Coverage Matrix: sc-cleanup-audit-protocol\n\n| Pattern | Required by Workflow? | Covering Step Design | Coverage Status |\n|---------|----------------------|---------------------|----------------|\n| Sequential step | Yes | G-001 → G-002 → G-003 → G-004 → G-005 → G-006 (topological order) | ✅ Covered |\n| Parallel operations | Yes | G-002, G-003 use ThreadPoolExecutor batch dispatch | ✅ Covered |\n| Quality gate | Yes | All 6 steps have GateCriteria defined (D-0023) | ✅ Covered |\n| Agent delegation | Yes | G-002 through G-006 use Claude subprocess prompts | ✅ Covered |\n| Scoring formula | Yes | 7 semantic check functions defined with `Callable[[str], bool]` | ✅ Covered |\n| Status decision | Yes | `determine_status()` classifies 8 exit conditions | ✅ Covered |\n| Input validation | Yes | `CleanupAuditConfig` validates target_path, batch_size, pass_filter | ✅ Covered |\n\n**Coverage result**: 7/7 patterns covered ✅\n**Gaps detected**: 0\n**Coverage complete**: true\n\n---\n\n## 6. Step Mapping Engine (FR-024)\n    11→\n    12→### Mapping Types\n    13→\n    14→The step mapping engine transforms source steps (from Phase 1 analysis) into generated steps (for code generation). Four mapping types are supported:\n    15→\n    16→| Mapping Type | Description | Justification Requirement |\n    17→|-------------|-------------|--------------------------|\n    18→| `1:1` | One source step maps to exactly one generated step | Optional — default mapping |\n    19→| `1:N` | One source step splits into N generated steps | Required — explain split rationale |\n    20→| `N:1` | N source steps merge into one generated step | Required — explain merge rationale |\n    21→| `1:0` | One source step is eliminated | Required — must provide elimination record |\n    22→\n    23→### Mapping Algorithm\n    24→\n    25→```\n    26→map_source_to_generated(\n    27→    source_steps: list[SourceStep],\n    28→    classified_steps: list[ClassifiedStep],\n    29→    dag: DependencyDAG,\n    30→    gate_assignments: list[GateAssignment]\n    31→) -> StepMappingResult\n    32→```\n    33→\n    34→**Process**:\n    35→1. For each source step `S-NNN`, determine the appropriate mapping type:\n    36→   - If the step translates directly to one generated step → `1:1`\n    37→   - If the step requires splitting (e.g., a batch operation with pre-batch and post-batch logic) → `1:N`\n    38→   - If multiple source steps share enough implementation that they should be a single generated step → `N:1`\n    39→   - If the step has no generated equivalent (e.g., absorbed into executor logic or eliminated) → `1:0`\n    40→2. Assign generated step IDs in format `G-NNN` (sequential, zero-padded to 3 digits)\n    41→3. Record justification for all non-1:1 mappings\n    42→4. For `1:0` mappings, create an elimination record\n    43→\n    44→### Generated Step ID Assignment\n    45→\n    46→```\n    47→assign_generated_ids(mappings: list[StepMapping]) -> list[StepMapping]\n    48→```\n    49→\n    50→Generated IDs are assigned sequentially based on the topological order of their source steps:\n    51→- `G-001`, `G-002`, ..., `G-NNN`\n    52→- For `1:N` splits, sub-IDs use the pattern `G-NNN` (each gets its own top-level ID)\n    53→- For `N:1` merges, the merged step gets a single `G-NNN` ID\n    54→- `1:0` eliminated steps receive no generated ID\n    55→\n    56→### Mapping Record Structure\n    57→\n    58→```yaml\n    59→step_mapping:\n    60→  - source_id: \"S-001\"           # Source step from Phase 1\n    61→    generated_step_ids: [\"G-001\"] # Generated step(s)\n    62→    mapping_type: \"1:1\"          # Mapping type\n    63→    justification: null          # Not required for 1:1\n    64→```\n    65→\n    66→---\n    67→\n    68→## 2. Elimination Records (FR-025)\n    69→\n    70→### Record Structure\n    71→\n    72→Steps mapped as `1:0` must have an elimination record with all three required fields:\n    73→\n    74→```yaml\n    75→elimination_records:\n    76→  - source_id: \"S-NNN\"          # Which source step was eliminated\n    77→    reason: \"<explanation>\"      # Why it was eliminated\n    78→    approved_by: \"auto\" | \"user\" # Who approved the elimination\n    79→```\n    80→\n    81→**Field requirements**:\n    82→- `source_id`: Must reference a valid source step ID from Phase 1 analysis (non-empty string matching `S-\\d{3}`)\n    83→- `reason`: Must be a non-empty string explaining why this step has no generated equivalent\n    84→- `approved_by`: Must be either `\"auto\"` (if the elimination is self-evident, e.g., step absorbed into executor overhead) or `\"user\"` (if the elimination required user review)\n    85→\n    86→### Auto-Approval Criteria\n    87→\n    88→An elimination may be auto-approved (`approved_by: \"auto\"`) when:\n    89→- The step's function is absorbed into the executor's built-in behavior (e.g., step sequencing, retry logic)\n    90→- The step is purely orchestrational with no domain-specific output\n    91→- The step's output is a subset of another step's output (deduplication)\n    92→\n    93→All other eliminations require `approved_by: \"user\"`.\n    94→\n    95→---\n    96→\n    97→## 3. Coverage Invariant Enforcement (FR-025, FR-049)\n    98→\n    99→### Invariant Equation\n   100→\n   101→```\n   102→|source_step_registry| == |mapped_steps| + |elimination_records|\n   103→```\n   104→\n   105→Where:\n   106→- `|source_step_registry|` = number of source steps from Phase 1 (the `source_step_count` from D-0017)\n   107→- `|mapped_steps|` = number of unique source steps that have at least one generated step mapping (mapping types 1:1, 1:N, or participating in N:1)\n   108→- `|elimination_records|` = number of `1:0` elimination records\n   109→\n   110→### Enforcement Algorithm\n   111→\n   112→```\n   113→enforce_coverage_invariant(\n   114→    source_steps: list[SourceStep],\n   115→    mappings: list[StepMapping],\n   116→    eliminations: list[EliminationRecord]\n   117→) -> CoverageInvariantResult\n   118→```\n   119→\n   120→1. Compute `source_count = len(source_steps)`\n   121→2. Compute `mapped_source_ids = set(m.source_id for m in mappings if m.mapping_type != \"1:0\")`\n   122→3. Compute `eliminated_source_ids = set(e.source_id for e in eliminations)`\n   123→4. Verify no overlap: `mapped_source_ids & eliminated_source_ids == {}`\n   124→5. Verify completeness: `mapped_source_ids | eliminated_source_ids == {s.source_id for s in source_steps}`\n   125→6. Verify count: `len(mapped_source_ids) + len(eliminated_source_ids) == source_count`\n   126→\n   127→**On violation**: The engine halts with a blocking error:\n   128→```\n   129→COVERAGE_INVARIANT_VIOLATION: Source step count (N) != mapped (M) + eliminated (E)\n   130→Missing source steps: [S-NNN, ...]\n   131→Duplicate mappings: [S-NNN, ...]\n   132→Action: Every source step must appear in exactly one mapping or elimination record.\n   133→```\n   134→\n   135→### Result Structure\n   136→\n   137→```yaml\n   138→coverage_invariant:\n   139→  source_step_count: 6           # |source_step_registry|\n   140→  mapped_step_count: 6           # |mapped_steps|\n   141→  eliminated_count: 0            # |elimination_records|\n   142→  invariant_holds: true          # source == mapped + eliminated\n   143→```\n   144→\n   145→---\n   146→\n   147→## 4. Pure-Programmatic Step Design (FR-029)\n   321→\n   322→### G-001: Discover and Classify Files\n   323→\n   324→This is the sole pure-programmatic step. Full Python code specification:\n   325→\n   326→```python\n   327→def run_discover_files(config: CleanupAuditConfig) -> None:\n   328→    \"\"\"\n   329→    G-001: Discover and classify files in the target repository.\n   330→\n   331→    Produces: {work_dir}/G-001-output.md\n   332→    Gate: LIGHT / BLOCKING\n   333→    \"\"\"\n   334→    target = config.target_path.resolve()\n   335→    output = config.work_dir / \"G-001-output.md\"\n   336→\n   337→    # 1. Walk the directory tree, respecting .gitignore\n   338→    all_files = []\n   339→    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(target):\n   340→        # Skip hidden dirs and common ignores\n   341→        dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if not d.startswith(\".\") and d not in {\"node_modules\", \"__pycache__\", \".git\"}]\n   342→        for f in files:\n   343→            rel_path = os.path.relpath(os.path.join(root, f), target)\n   344→            ext = os.path.splitext(f)[1]\n   345→            size = os.path.getsize(os.path.join(root, f))\n   346→            all_files.append({\n   347→                \"path\": rel_path,\n   348→                \"extension\": ext,\n   349→                \"size_bytes\": size,\n   350→            })\n   351→\n   352→    # 2. Classify by extension into categories\n   353→    categories = {\n   354→        \"code\": {\".py\", \".ts\", \".tsx\", \".js\", \".jsx\", \".go\", \".rs\", \".java\"},\n   355→        \"config\": {\".yaml\", \".yml\", \".json\", \".toml\", \".ini\", \".cfg\"},\n   356→        \"docs\": {\".md\", \".rst\", \".txt\"},\n   357→        \"test\": set(),  # Identified by path patterns\n   358→        \"other\": set(),\n   359→    }\n   360→\n   361→    for f in all_files:\n   362→        if \"test\" in f[\"path\"].lower() or f[\"path\"].startswith(\"tests/\"):\n   363→            f[\"category\"] = \"test\"\n   364→        elif f[\"extension\"] in categories[\"code\"]:\n   365→            f[\"category\"] = \"code\"\n   366→        elif f[\"extension\"] in categories[\"config\"]:\n   367→            f[\"category\"] = \"config\"\n   368→        elif f[\"extension\"] in categories[\"docs\"]:\n   369→            f[\"category\"] = \"docs\"\n   370→        else:\n   371→            f[\"category\"] = \"other\"\n   372→\n   373→    # 3. Write output\n   374→    with open(output, \"w\") as fh:\n   375→        fh.write(\"---\\n\")\n   376→        fh.write(f\"title: File Discovery Inventory\\n\")\n   377→        fh.write(f\"status: complete\\n\")\n   378→        fh.write(f\"total_files: {len(all_files)}\\n\")\n   379→        fh.write(\"---\\n\\n\")\n   380→        fh.write(\"# File Inventory\\n\\n\")\n   381→        fh.write(\"| Path | Extension | Size | Category |\\n\")\n   382→        fh.write(\"|------|-----------|------|----------|\\n\")\n   383→        for f in sorted(all_files, key=lambda x: x[\"path\"]):\n   384→            fh.write(f\"| {f['path']} | {f['extension']} | {f['size_bytes']} | {f['category']} |\\n\")\n   385→        fh.write(f\"\\n## Summary\\n\\n\")\n   386→        for cat in [\"code\", \"test\", \"config\", \"docs\", \"other\"]:\n   387→            count = sum(1 for f in all_files if f[\"category\"] == cat)\n   388→            fh.write(f\"- **{cat}**: {count} files\\n\")\n   389→```\n   390→\n   391→**PROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS registration**:\n   392→```python\n   393→PROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS = {\n   394→    \"G-001\": run_discover_files,\n   395→}\n   396→```\n   397→\n   398→---\n   399→\n   400→## 4. Executor Design (FR-030)\n   401→\n   402→### 4.1 Architecture: Sprint-Style Synchronous Supervisor\n   403→\n   404→The executor follows the sprint-style supervisor loop pattern from pipeline-spec.md:\n   405→- **Synchronous** supervisor loop (not async/await)\n   406→- **ThreadPoolExecutor** for batch dispatch of parallel steps (S-002, S-003)\n   407→- **time.sleep()** polling for subprocess monitoring\n   408→- **TurnLedger** for budget management (from `superclaude.cli.sprint.models`)\n   409→\n   410→### 4.2 Executor Pseudocode\n   411→\n   412→```python\n   413→def execute_cleanup_audit(config: CleanupAuditConfig) -> AuditResult:\n   414→    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n   415→    verify_claude_binary()\n   416→\n   417→    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n   418→    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n   419→    ledger = TurnLedger(\n   420→        initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n   421→        minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n   422→        minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n   423→    )\n   424→    result = AuditResult(config=config)\n   425→\n   426→    try:\n   427→        # Step ordering follows topological sort from D-0018:\n   428→        # G-001 → G-002 → G-003 → G-004 → G-005 → G-006\n   429→\n   430→        # --- G-001: Pure programmatic (discover files) ---\n   431→        step_result = run_programmatic_step(\"G-001\", config)\n   432→        result.add(step_result)\n   433→        if step_result.status != AuditStepStatus.PASS:\n   434→            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n   435→            return result\n   436→\n   437→        # --- G-002: Claude-assisted batch (surface scan) ---\n   438→        file_inventory = parse_inventory(config.work_dir / \"G-001-output.md\")\n   439→        batches = create_batches(file_inventory, config.batch_size)\n   440→\n   441→        for batch_idx, batch in enumerate(batches):\n   442→            if not ledger.can_launch():\n   443→                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n   444→                result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n   445→                return result\n   446→\n   447→            step_result = run_claude_step(\n   448→                step_id=f\"G-002\",\n   449→                prompt=build_surface_scan_prompt(batch, config),\n   450→                gate=G002_GATE,\n   451→                gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n   452→                config=config,\n   453→                ledger=ledger,\n   454→            )\n   455→            result.add(step_result)\n   456→            if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n   457→                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n   458→                return result\n   459→\n   460→        # --- G-003: Claude-assisted batch (structural analysis) ---\n   461→        review_files = extract_review_files(config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\")\n   462→        batches = create_batches(review_files, config.batch_size)\n   463→\n   464→        for batch_idx, batch in enumerate(batches):\n   465→            if not ledger.can_launch():\n   466→                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n   467→                return result\n   468→\n   469→            step_result = run_claude_step(\n   470→                step_id=f\"G-003\",\n   471→                prompt=build_structural_analysis_prompt(\n   472→                    batch, config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\", config\n   473→                ),\n   474→                gate=G003_GATE,\n   475→                gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n   476→                config=config,\n   477→                ledger=ledger,\n   478→            )\n   479→            result.add(step_result)\n   480→            if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n   481→                result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n   482→                return result\n   483→\n   484→        # --- G-004: Claude-assisted single (cross-cutting) ---\n   485→        if not ledger.can_launch():\n   486→            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n   487→            return result\n   488→\n   489→        step_result = run_claude_step(\n   490→            step_id=\"G-004\",\n   491→            prompt=build_cross_cutting_prompt(\n   492→                config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\",\n   493→                config.work_dir / \"G-003-output.md\",\n   494→                config,\n   495→            ),\n   496→            gate=G004_GATE,\n   497→            gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n   498→            config=config,\n   499→            ledger=ledger,\n   500→        )\n   501→        result.add(step_result)\n   502→        if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n   503→            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n   504→            return result\n   505→\n   506→        # --- G-005: Claude-assisted single (consolidate) ---\n   507→        if not ledger.can_launch():\n   508→            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n   509→            return result\n   510→\n   511→        step_result = run_claude_step(\n   512→            step_id=\"G-005\",\n   513→            prompt=build_consolidation_prompt(\n   514→                config.work_dir / \"G-002-output.md\",\n   515→                config.work_dir / \"G-003-output.md\",\n   516→                config.work_dir / \"G-004-output.md\",\n   517→                config,\n   518→            ),\n   519→            gate=G005_GATE,\n   520→            gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,\n   521→            config=config,\n   522→            ledger=ledger,\n   523→        )\n   524→        result.add(step_result)\n   525→        if step_result.status not in (AuditStepStatus.PASS, AuditStepStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n   526→            result.outcome = \"HALTED\"\n   527→            return result\n   528→\n   529→        # --- G-006: Claude-assisted single (validate — TRAILING) ---\n   530→        if not ledger.can_launch():\n   531→            # Trailing step — budget exhaustion is advisory, not blocking\n   532→            result.add_advisory(\"G-006 skipped: budget exhausted\")\n   533→        else:\n   534→            step_result = run_claude_step(\n   535→                step_id=\"G-006\",\n   536→                prompt=build_validation_prompt(\n   537→                    config.work_dir / \"G-005-output.md\",\n   538→                    sample_findings(config.work_dir / \"G-005-output.md\"),\n   539→                    config,\n   540→                ),\n   541→                gate=G006_GATE,\n   542→                gate_mode=GateMode.TRAILING,\n   543→                config=config,\n   544→                ledger=ledger,\n   545→            )\n   546→            result.add(step_result)\n   547→            # TRAILING: pipeline continues regardless of gate result\n   548→\n   549→        result.outcome = \"PASSED\"\n   550→        return result\n   551→\n   552→    finally:\n   553→        signal_handler.restore()\n   554→```\n   555→\n   556→### 4.3 Batch Dispatch with ThreadPoolExecutor\n   557→\n   558→For steps that process batches (G-002, G-003), the executor uses `ThreadPoolExecutor` when batches are independent:\n   559→\n   560→```python\n   561→from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed\n   562→\n   563→def execute_parallel_batches(\n   564→    batches: list[list[str]],\n   565→    build_prompt_fn: callable,\n   566→    gate: GateCriteria,\n   567→    config: CleanupAuditConfig,\n   568→    ledger: TurnLedger,\n   569→    max_workers: int = 3,\n   570→) -> list[AuditStepResult]:\n   571→    \"\"\"Execute independent batches in parallel using ThreadPoolExecutor.\"\"\"\n   572→    results = []\n   573→\n   574→    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=max_workers) as executor:\n   575→        futures = {}\n   576→        for batch_idx, batch in enumerate(batches):\n   577→            if not ledger.can_launch():\n   578→                break\n   579→            future = executor.submit(\n   580→                run_claude_step,\n   581→                step_id=f\"batch-{batch_idx}\",\n   582→                prompt=build_prompt_fn(batch, config),\n   583→                gate=gate,\n   584→                config=config,\n   585→                ledger=ledger,\n   586→            )\n   587→            futures[future] = batch_idx\n   588→\n   589→        for future in as_completed(futures):\n   590→            batch_idx = futures[future]\n   591→            result = future.result()\n   592→            results.append(result)\n   593→\n   594→    return sorted(results, key=lambda r: r.batch_index)\n   595→```\n   596→\n   597→---\n   598→\n   599→## 5.
